 - Rajnath Singh (@rajnathsingh) October 7, 2019 Arms worship tradition has been in place in India for a long time
 maharana pratap kii is dharti par rajput raja dushmano ko ranbhumi main chakke chhudaane se pehle astr-shastr kii puja karte rahe hai

 Vijayadashami was celebrated on the tenth day of the Shukla Paksha of Ashwin month
 isi din bhagwaan ram ne lanka ke raja ravan par vijay praapt kii thi

 The coincidence of the numbers associated with Vajpayee's birth and death was strange
 unke janm kii taarikh or maran kii taarikh kaa jod ek hi sankhya thi yani unke janm kii taarikh kii sankhyaon ko jodakar maran kii taarikh kii sankhyaon ke yoga se gata diya jaae, to shunya aata he
 The same void in which Bharat Ratna Atal Bihari Vajpayee merged into perpetual sleep
 atal bihari vaajapeyika janm madhya pradesh ke gwalior main 25 disambar 1924 yani 25-12-1924 taarikh ko hua tha
 If the digits of this date are added, then 2 + 5 + 1 + 2 + 1 + 9 + 2 + 4 = 26
 isi tarah unke nidhan kii taarikh 16-08-2018 yani 16 agast 2018 ke ankon ko joda jaae, to 1+6+0+8+2+0+1+8 = 26 sankhya aati he
 In this way, the sum of the digits of Vajpayee's date of birth and death comes to 26-26
 agar in donon sankhyaon ko aapas main gata diya jaae, to shunya aata he yani 26-26 = 00 (shunya)
 In regard to the birth and death of former Prime Minister Vajpayee, zero proved to be the absolute truth

 Apart from this, the sum of the date of birth of Atal Bihari Vajpayee is also strange
 unka janm maheene kii 25 taarikh or dehanth 16 taarikh ko hua tha

e
 2 + 5 = 7 and 1 + 6 = 7
